donna_32.h
1// donna_32.h - written and placed in public domain by Jeffrey Walton
2// Crypto++ specific implementation wrapped around Andrew
3// Moon's public domain curve25519-donna and ed25519-donna,
4// https://github.com/floodyberry/curve25519-donna and
5// https://github.com/floodyberry/ed25519-donna.
6
7// This source file multiplexes two different repos using namespaces. This
8// was a little easier from a project management standpoint. We only need
9// two files per architecture at the expense of namespaces and bloat.
10
11#ifndef CRYPTOPP_DONNA_32_H
12#define CRYPTOPP_DONNA_32_H
13#ifndef CRYPTOPP_DOXYGEN_PROCESSING
14
15#include "config.h"
16
17NAMESPACE_BEGIN(CryptoPP)
18NAMESPACE_BEGIN(Donna)
19NAMESPACE_BEGIN(Arch32)
20
21using CryptoPP::byte;
22using CryptoPP::word32;
23using CryptoPP::word64;
24
25// ******************** x25519 Agreement ************************* //
26
27#define ALIGN(n) CRYPTOPP_ALIGN_DATA(n)
28#define mul32x32_64(a,b) (((word64)(a))*(b))
29
30typedef word32 bignum25519[10];
31
32const byte basePoint[32] = {9};
33const word32 reduce_mask_25 = (1 << 25) - 1;
34const word32 reduce_mask_26 = (1 << 26) - 1;
35
36// ****************** ed25519 Signatures *********************** //
37
38typedef byte hash_512bits[64];
39
40const int bignum256modm_bits_per_limb = 30;
41const int bignum256modm_limb_size = 9;
42typedef word32 bignum256modm_element_t;
43typedef bignum256modm_element_t bignum256modm[9];
44
45struct ge25519 {
46 bignum25519 x, y, z, t;
47};
48
49struct ge25519_p1p1 {
50 bignum25519 x, y, z, t;
51};
52
53struct ge25519_niels {
54 bignum25519 ysubx, xaddy, t2d;
55};
56
57struct ge25519_pniels {
58 bignum25519 ysubx, xaddy, z, t2d;
59};
60
61#define S1_SWINDOWSIZE 5
62#define S1_TABLE_SIZE (1<<(S1_SWINDOWSIZE-2))
63#define S2_SWINDOWSIZE 7
64#define S2_TABLE_SIZE (1<<(S2_SWINDOWSIZE-2))
65
